NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
	
T. Lokesh,  a male child, son of Thiru K. Thennarasu, born on 25th June 1998, residing at 
No. 23C, K Manikkam Street, Senkunram, Madhavaram Taluk, Naravarikuppam, Chennai-600 052, has been living 
as a Transwomen.  I have been Granted Identity  Card No. TG03075, issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, 
Social Welfare and NMP Department.  By this, I may be treated as a Transwomen and shall henceforth be known as T. OVIYA.
Chennai, 	
T. LOKESH
5th July 2022. 
	
I.  Farook,  a male child, son of Thiru Ismail, born on 10th October 1999, residing at No. 495, P Block West 
Cementry Road, Old Washermenpet, Chennai-600 021, has been living as Transwomen. I have been Granted 
Identity  Card No. CHN/015/2019,  issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board.  Social Welfare and NMP Department. 
By this, I may be treated as a Transwomen and  shall henceforth be known as I. YASHIKA.
Chennai, 	
I. FAROOK
